016073,003141:                                                                                                  #                                          FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
016074,003142:    4220           34674        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #     THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
016075,003143:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
016076,003144:                                                                                                  #                                           MONITOR BIT.
016077,003145:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016078,003146: 
016079,003147: 
016080,003148:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
016081,003149:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016082,003150:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
016083,003151:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
016084,003152:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
016085,003153: 
016086,003154: 
016087,003155:                                                                                                  #  L  TC ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
016088,003156:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
016089,003157:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
016090,003158:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016091,003159:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016092,003160:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
016093,003161:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
016094,003162:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
016095,003163:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
016096,003164:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
016097,003165:

Page 365 

016099,003167: 
016100,003168:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
016101,003169:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
016102,003170:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
016103,003171:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016104,003172:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
016105,003173:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
016106,003174: 
016107,003175:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
016108,003176:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
016109,003177:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
016110,003178:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
016111,003179:    4227           74747                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
016112,003180:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
016113,003181:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
016114,003182:    4232           05070                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016115,003183:

016465,003533:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016466,003534: 
016467,003535:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016468,003536:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016469,003537:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016470,003538:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016471,003539: 
016472,003540:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016473,003541:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
016474,003542:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
016475,003543:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016476,003544:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016477,003545:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016478,003546:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016479,003547: 
016480,003548: 
016481,003549:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016482,003550:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
016483,003551:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
016484,003552:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016485,003553:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016486,003554: 
016487,003555: 
016488,003556:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
016489,003557:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016490,003558:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016491,003559:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016492,003560:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016493,003561: 
016494,003562: 
016495,003563:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016496,003564:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
016497,003565:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
016498,003566: 
016499,003567: 
016500,003568:                                                                                                  #  .
016501,003569: 
016502,003570: 
016503,003571:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016504,003572:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
016505,003573:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016506,003574:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016507,003575: 
016508,003576: 
016509,003577:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016510,003578:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016511,003579:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016512,003580:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016513,003581:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
016514,003582:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 374 

016516,003584:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016517,003585: 
016518,003586:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016519,003587:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
016520,003588:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016521,003589:    4456           04574        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016522,003590:    4457           10550                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016523,003591:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016524,003592: 
016525,003593:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016526,003594:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016527,003595: 
016528,003596: 04,2550                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016529,003597: 04,2550                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016530,003598: 
016531,003599: 04,2550           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016532,003600: 04,2551           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016533,003601: 04,2552           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016534,003602: 04,2553           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016535,003603: 04,2554           30001                           CA       L                                     
016536,003604: 04,2555           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016537,003605: 04,2556           05070        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016538,003606: 
016539,003607: 
016540,003608:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016541,003609:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016542,003610:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016543,003611:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016544,003612:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016545,003613: 
016546,003614:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016547,003615:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016548,003616: 
016549,003617:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016550,003618:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016551,003619:    4463           34675                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016552,003620:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016553,003621:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016554,003622:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016555,003623:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016556,003624:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016557,003625:                                                                                                  #                                          AFTER EXECUTION.
016558,003626:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016559,003627:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016560,003628: 
016561,003629: 
016562,003630:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016563,003631:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016564,003632:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016565,003633:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT

Page 375 

016567,003635:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF,  SEARCH DSPLIST
016568,003636:    4475           44675                           CS       BIT14                                 
016569,003637:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016570,003638:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016571,003639:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016572,003640:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016573,003641:    4502           04504                           TC       +2

016703,003771:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016704,003772:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016705,003773:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016706,003774:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016707,003775:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
016708,003776:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016709,003777:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.

016715,003783: 40,3505           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.
